<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">оде́сса</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Odéssa, odɛ́ssa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Odessa</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***одеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a> (10739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oděti</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">detʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dress, to clothe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теплый.html>тепло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">detéj <b>odéli</b> tepló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the children had been <b>dressed</b> warmly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to provide clothes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедняга.html>бедня́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накормить.html>накорми́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bednjágu nádo nakormítʹ i <b>odétʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the poor fellow needs to be fed and <b>given clothes</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1833</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a>. Пушкин (Alexander Pushkin),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>О́сень</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> багре́ц <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одетый.html>оде́тые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V bagréc i zóloto <b>odétyje</b> lesá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Woods <b>covered</b> in crimson and gold</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put on <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">clothing, equipment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шапка.html>ша́пку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>odél</b> na gólovu šápku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he <b>put on</b> a hat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Usage of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a> (что-либо)</b> in the sense of <i>to put on (something)</i> is considered non-standard in modern Russian; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеть.html>наде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should be used instead.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***одеяло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеяло.html>одеяло</a> (1986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">одѣꙝло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oděꙝlo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">garment, blanket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">одѣꙗло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odějalo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">outerwear, cloak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">дѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">děti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set, to place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*děti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeh₁-</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">face</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">do</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяло.html>одея́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odejálo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяло.html>одея́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяло.html>одея́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяло.html>одея́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blanket, counterpane</li>
<li>quilt</li></ol>

***одеяние.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ние</a> (12333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">одѣѩиѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odějęije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odejánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеяние.html>одея́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> raiment, attire, garb, habiliments <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually festive, solemn</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***один.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> (3179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*edinъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*óynos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, single</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>one (1)
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odín</b> málʹčik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one boy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹdesját <b>odín</b> málʹčik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fifty-one boys</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">fifty-one boy</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odná</b> kníga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>Здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zdesʹ pjatʹdesját <b>odná</b> kníga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Here are fifty-one books</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Here (is) fifty-one book</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V mojóm dóme jestʹ dvádcatʹ <b>odnó</b> bolʹšóje oknó</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There are twenty-one large windows in my house.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">In my house there is twenty-one large window.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V mojóm dóme býlo dvádcatʹ <b>odnó</b> bolʹšóje oknó</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There were twenty-one large windows in my house.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">In my house there was twenty-one large window.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>alone</li>
<li>only (especially with negative connotation)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодильник.html>холоди́льнике</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́лись</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:консервы.html>консе́рвы</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V xolodílʹnike ostálisʹ <b>odní</b> konsérvy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There’s nothing but cans left in the refrigerator.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a, a certain, some
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прочитать.html>прочита́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ге</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja pročitál éto v <b>odnój</b> kníge.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I read it in some book.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni <b>odín</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not a single</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курс.html>курс</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:записаться.html>записа́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:студент.html>студе́нт</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na kurs ne zapisálsja ni <b>odín</b> studént.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Not a single student has subscribed to the course.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>нашёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>сту́ла</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vo vsjóm dóme ja ne našól ni <b>odnovó</b> stúla.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I haven't found not a single chair in the entire house.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">modern slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni <b>odná</b> sobáka</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">no one <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">often about people who don't care about somebody</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">not a single dog</span>”)</dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́цах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инфаркт.html>инфа́рктами</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>Ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вспомнить.html>вспо́мнила</a>! (<a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>Из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:интервью.html>интервью́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> Михаилом Кононовым)</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kogdá (ja) četýre goda nazád ležál v bolʹnícax s infárktami, nikomú do menjá dela né bylo. Ni <b>odná</b> sobáka (obo mne) ne vspómnila! (Iz intɛrvʹjú s Mixailom Kononovym)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">When I was lying in the hospital with heart attack four years ago, no one cared about me. No one remembered about it!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">contrast</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> some (do something or have some quality), while others (do not do it; do something else; do not have this quality; or have another or the opposite quality)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:биолог.html>био́логи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ют</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́русы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произойти.html>произошли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бактерия.html>бакте́рий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>ни́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:согласный.html>согла́сны</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Odní</b> biólogi sčitájut, što vírusy proizošlí ot baktérij/baktɛ́rij, drugíje s ními ne soglásny</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Some biologists believe that viruses evolved from bacteria, while others disagree.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:насекомое.html>насеко́мые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крылатый.html>крыла́ты</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишенный.html>лишены́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́льев</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Odní</b> nasekómyje kryláty, drugíje lišený krýlʹjev</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Some insects are winged, others have no wings.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одни́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быко́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стадо.html>ста́де</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кастрировать.html>кастри́ровали</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Odníx</b> bykóv v stáde kastrírovali, drugíx ješčó net</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Some bulls in the herd were castrated, others not yet.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́е</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Odní</b> govorját <b>odnó</b>, drugíje drugóje</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There are contradictory rumours about the topic.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whether alone or in compounds (21, 31, 41, 101, etc.), govern the singular. All intervening adjectives and adjectival participles also become singular. If the noun is in nominative case, the corresponding verb also becomes singular.</li></ul>

***одиннадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцать.html>оди́ннадцать</a> (3414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дцать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or "one on ten". The final syllable <b>-дцать</b> is an old short form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">désjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцать.html>оди́ннадцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odínnadcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eleven (11)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцать.html>оди́ннадцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odinnadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцать.html>оди́ннадцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odínnadcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eleven boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцать.html>оди́ннадцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>odínnadcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with eleven boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцать.html>оди́ннадцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>odínnadcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately eleven boys</span></div></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одинокий.html>одино́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odinókij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)одино́че</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>solitary, single, lone</li>
<li>lonely, lonesome</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чный</a> (11508)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odinóčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>single
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чный</a></b> полёт</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odinóčnyj</b> poljót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">solo flight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостиница.html>гости́нице</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odinóčnyj</b> nómer (v gostínice)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">single room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odinóčnoje</b> zaključénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">solitary confinement</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:катание.html>ката́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конька́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odinóčnoje</b> katánije na konʹkáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">single skating; singles</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odinóčnyj</b> ogónʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">individual fire; single-round firing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***одиозный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одиозный.html>одио́зный</a> (29167)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed during the second half of the 19th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">odieux</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">odiōsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиозный.html>одио́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odióznyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)одио́знее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)одио́зней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>odious, extremely unpleasant</li></ol>

***одичать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одичать.html>одича́ть</a> (16346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дича́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dičátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одичать.html>одича́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odičátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дича́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run wild</li>
<li>to become wild, to grow wild</li>
<li>to become shy or unsociable</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***однажды.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a> (591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жды</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ždy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odnáždy</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>once, one day, once upon a time
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  N. A. Nekrasov,  <cite>Russian Peasant Children</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:студеный.html>студёную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зимний.html>зи́мнюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́ру</a>…</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Odnáždy</b> v studjónuju zímnjuju póru…</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Once on a cold wintry day…</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:побывать.html>побыва́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снова.html>сно́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вернуться.html>вернётесь</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odnáždy</b> pobyváv tam, vy snóva tudá vernjótesʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">having once visited that place, you'll come back again</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>once (only one time)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живёшь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">živjóšʹ tólʹko <b>odnáždy</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">you only live once</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">one day</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ка́к-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kák-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ка́к-то <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kák-to raz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некогда.html>не́когда</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nékogda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>colloq.</i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only one time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единожды.html>еди́ножды</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedínoždy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>colloq.</i>)</li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:однокашник.html>однока́шник</a> (14889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">одно-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odno-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">káša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the old dialectal meaning "joint meal, voluntary association/society" of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каша.html>ка́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">káša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одобрительный.html>одобри́тельный</a> (21831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одобрить.html>одо́брить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odóbritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одобрительный.html>одобри́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odobrítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>approving, approbative</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одобрять.html>одобря́ть</a> (8078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóbryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одобрять.html>одобря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odobrjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одобрить.html>одо́брить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to approbate, to approve, to pass, to sanction, to authorize
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1972</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%94%D0%BC%D0%B8%D1%82%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%A1%D1%83%D1%85%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B2" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Дмитрий Сухарев">Дмитрий Сухарев</a></span> (Dmitri Sukharev) (lyrics), <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Viktor_Berkovsky" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Viktor Berkovsky">Viktor Berkovsky</a> (music),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ку</a> Тябу</span>  | Song about the Dog Tyaba | ”:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> ва́ся <a href = vnd.unilang:вместе.html>вме́сте</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>не́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одобрять.html>одобря́ет</a></b>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собачка.html>соба́чка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вку</a> удобря́ет.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I Vásja vméste s néj ne <b>odobrjájet</b>, / Kogdá sobáčka trávku udobrjájet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And Vasya, together with her, <b>does</b> not <b>approve</b>, / When the dog fertilizes the grass.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
